"""FP8 e4m3 GEMM kernel using CUDA C++ with nvcuda::wmma (bf16 tensor cores).
Converts fp8→bf16 on-the-fly during global→shared load, then uses bf16 WMMA.
"""
import torch
import torch.nn as nn

# CUDA kernel source
CUDA_SRC = r"""
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_fp8.h>
#include <mma.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

constexpr int BM = 32;
constexpr int BN = 64;
constexpr int BK = 32;
constexpr int WARPS_M = BM / 16;
constexpr int WARPS_N = BN / 16;
constexpr int NUM_WARPS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N;
constexpr int THREADS = NUM_WARPS * 32;

__global__ void fp8_gemm_kernel(
    const __nv_fp8_e4m3* __restrict__ A,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ B,
    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ C,
    int M, int N, int K
) {
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_A[BM * BK];
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_B[BN * BK];

    int warp_id = threadIdx.x / 32;
    int warp_m = warp_id % WARPS_M;
    int warp_n = warp_id / WARPS_M;

    int block_row = blockIdx.x * BM;
    int block_col = blockIdx.y * BN;

    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> frag_a;
    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, col_major> frag_b;
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
    fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);

    for (int k = 0; k < K; k += BK) {
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_row + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            float fval;
            if (g_row < M && g_col < K) {
                fval = (float)A[g_row * K + g_col];
            } else {
                fval = 0.0f;
            }
            smem_A[row * BK + col] = __float2bfloat16(fval);
        }

        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BN * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_col + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            __nv_bfloat16 val;
            if (g_row < N && g_col < K) {
                val = B[g_row * K + g_col];
            } else {
                val = __float2bfloat16(0.0f);
            }
            smem_B[row * BK + col] = val;
        }

        __syncthreads();

        for (int kk = 0; kk < BK; kk += 16) {
            load_matrix_sync(frag_a, &smem_A[warp_m * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            load_matrix_sync(frag_b, &smem_B[warp_n * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            mma_sync(frag_c, frag_a, frag_b, frag_c);
        }

        __syncthreads();
    }

    {
        __shared__ float smem_float[BM * BN];
        store_matrix_sync(
            &smem_float[warp_m * 16 * BN + warp_n * 16],
            frag_c, BN, mem_row_major
        );
        __syncthreads();

        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BN; idx += THREADS) {
            int m = idx / BN;
            int n = idx % BN;
            int g_m = block_row + m;
            int g_n = block_col + n;
            if (g_m < M && g_n < N) {
                C[g_m * N + g_n] = __float2bfloat16(smem_float[m * BN + n]);
            }
        }
    }
}

extern "C" void launch_gemm(long long A, long long B, long long C, int M, int N, int K) {
    dim3 grid((M + BM - 1) / BM, (N + BN - 1) / BN);
    dim3 block(THREADS);
    fp8_gemm_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(
        reinterpret_cast<const __nv_fp8_e4m3*>(static_cast<uintptr_t>(A)),
        reinterpret_cast<const __nv_bfloat16*>(static_cast<uintptr_t>(B)),
        reinterpret_cast<__nv_bfloat16*>(static_cast<uintptr_t>(C)),
        M, N, K
    );
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
}
"""

# Compile once at module load time
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

_ext = load_inline(
    name="fp8_gemm_sm120",
    cpp_sources='extern "C" void launch_gemm(long long A, long long B, long long C, int M, int N, int K);',
    cuda_sources=CUDA_SRC,
    extra_cuda_cflags=["-arch=sm_120", "-O3", "--expt-relaxed-constexpr"],
    functions=["launch_gemm"],
    verbose=False,
)


OP_TYPE = "gemm"
SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["fp8_e4m3"]
HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, M: int, N: int, K: int):
        super().__init__()
        self.M, self.N, self.K = M, N, K
        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        nn.init.normal_(self.weight, std=0.02)

    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        out = torch.empty(self.M, self.N, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=x.device)
        _ext.launch_gemm(
            x.data_ptr(),
            self.weight.data_ptr(),
            out.data_ptr(),
            self.M, self.N, self.K,
        )
        return out


M = 4096
N = 4096
K = 4096


def get_inputs():
    x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
    return [x]


def get_init_inputs():
    return [M, N, K]

command (814 chars)
uv run python -c "
import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

# Test if wmma with fp8 compiles on SM120
cuda_test = '''
#include <mma.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

__global__ void test_wmma() {
    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_fp8_e4m3, row_major> a_frag;
    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_fp8_e4m3, col_major> b_frag;
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> c_frag;
    fill_fragment(c_frag, 0.0f);
}

void run_test() {
    test_wmma<<<1, 256>>>();
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
}
'''

mod = load_inline(
    name='test_wmma_fp8',
    cpp_sources='void run_test();',
    cuda_sources=cuda_test,
    extra_cuda_cflags=['-arch=sm_120', '-O3'],
    functions=['run_test'],
    verbose=False,
)

mod.run_test()
print('WMMA FP8 test passed!')
" 2>&1

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

# Test fp8 to bf16 conversion in CUDA, then wmma with bf16
cuda_test = '''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <mma.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

__global__ void test_kernel(const __nv_fp8_e4m3* A, __nv_bfloat16* smem, int N) {
    // Test fp8 to bf16 conversion
    __nv_fp8_e4m3 val = A[threadIdx.x];
    __nv_bfloat16 bf = __nv_fp8_e4m3_to_bfloat16(val);
    smem[threadIdx.x] = bf;
    
    // Test wmma fragments with bf16 from shared memory
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 tile[32];
    tile[threadIdx.x] = bf;
    __syncthreads();
    
    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> a_frag;
    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> b_frag;
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> c_frag;
    fill_fragment(c_frag, 0.0f);
    
    // Just test compilation - don't run (would need proper tile size)
}

void run_test() {
    __nv_fp8_e4m3* d_A;
    __nv_bfloat16* d_smem;
    cudaMalloc(&d_A, 256);
    cudaMalloc(&d_smem, 256 * 2);
    test_kernel<<<1, 256>>>(d_A, d_smem, 256);
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    cudaFree(d_A);
    cudaFree(d_smem);
}
'''

#include <cuda_fp8.h>

__global__ void test_kernel(const __nv_fp8_e4m3* A, float* out, int N) {

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cuda_test = '''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_fp8.h>
#include <mma.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

constexpr int BM = 32;
constexpr int BN = 64;
constexpr int BK = 32;
constexpr int THREADS = 256;

__global__ void fp8_gemm_kernel(
    const __nv_fp8_e4m3* __restrict__ A,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ B,
    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ C,
    int M, int N, int K
) {
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_A[BM * BK];
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_B[BN * BK];
    
    int warp_id = threadIdx.x / 32;
    int warp_m = warp_id % (BM / 16);
    int warp_n = warp_id / (BM / 16);
    
    int block_row = blockIdx.x * BM;
    int block_col = blockIdx.y * BN;
    
    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> frag_a;
    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, col_major> frag_b;
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
    fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);
    
    for (int k = 0; k < K; k += BK) {
        // Load A tile: fp8 -> bf16 conversion
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_row + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            __nv_fp8_e4m3 val = (g_row < M && g_col < K) ? A[g_row * K + g_col] : __nv_fp8_e4m3(0);
            float fval = (float)val;
            smem_A[row * BK + col] = __float2bfloat16(fval);
        }
        
        // Load B tile: bf16 (direct copy)
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BN * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_col + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            __nv_bfloat16 val = (g_row < N && g_col < K) ? B[g_row * K + g_col] : __nv_bfloat16(0);
            smem_B[row * BK + col] = val;
        }
        
        __syncthreads();
        
        for (int kk = 0; kk < BK; kk += 16) {
            load_matrix_sync(frag_a, &smem_A[warp_m * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            load_matrix_sync(frag_b, &smem_B[warp_n * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            mma_sync(frag_c, frag_a, frag_b, frag_c);
        }
        
        __syncthreads();
    }
    
    // Store result: convert float accumulator to bf16
    {
        __shared__ float smem_float[BM * BN];
        store_matrix_sync(
            &smem_float[warp_m * 16 * BN + warp_n * 16],
            frag_c, BN, mem_row_major
        );
        __syncthreads();
        
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BN; idx += THREADS) {
            int m = idx / BN;
            int n = idx % BN;
            int g_m = block_row + m;
            int g_n = block_col + n;
            if (g_m < M && g_n < N) {
                C[g_m * N + g_n] = __float2bfloat16(smem_float[m * BN + n]);
            }
        }
    }
}

void launch_gemm(const __nv_fp8_e4m3* A, const __nv_bfloat16* B, __nv_bfloat16* C, int M, int N, int K) {
    dim3 grid((M + BM - 1) / BM, (N + BN - 1) / BN);
    dim3 block(THREADS);
    fp8_gemm_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(A, B, C, M, N, K);
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
}
'''

mod = load_inline(
    name='test_full_gemm',
    cpp_sources='void launch_gemm(const __nv_fp8_e4m3*, const __nv_bfloat16*, __nv_bfloat16*, int, int, int);',
    cuda_sources=cuda_test,
    extra_cuda_cflags=['-arch=sm_120', '-O3', '--expt-relaxed-constexpr'],
    functions=['launch_gemm'],
    verbose=False,
)

# Test with small sizes
M, N, K = 32, 32, 32
A = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()

ref = A.to(torch.bfloat16) @ B.T
print('Max diff:', (C - ref).abs().max().item())
print('Test ' + ('PASSED' if torch.allclose(C, ref, atol=0.15, rtol=0.15) else 'FAILED'))

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cuda_test = '''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <cuda_fp8.h>
#include <mma.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

constexpr int BM = 32;
constexpr int BN = 64;
constexpr int BK = 32;
constexpr int WARPS_M = BM / 16;
constexpr int WARPS_N = BN / 16;
constexpr int NUM_WARPS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N;
constexpr int THREADS = NUM_WARPS * 32;

__global__ void fp8_gemm_kernel(
    const __nv_fp8_e4m3* __restrict__ A,
    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ B,
    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ C,
    int M, int N, int K
) {
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_A[BM * BK];
    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_B[BN * BK];
    
    int warp_id = threadIdx.x / 32;
    int warp_m = warp_id % WARPS_M;
    int warp_n = warp_id / WARPS_M;
    
    int block_row = blockIdx.x * BM;
    int block_col = blockIdx.y * BN;
    
    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> frag_a;
    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, col_major> frag_b;
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
    fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);
    
    for (int k = 0; k < K; k += BK) {
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_row + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            float fval;
            if (g_row < M && g_col < K) {
                fval = (float)A[g_row * K + g_col];
            } else {
                fval = 0.0f;
            }
            smem_A[row * BK + col] = __float2bfloat16(fval);
        }
        
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BN * BK; idx += THREADS) {
            int row = idx / BK;
            int col = idx % BK;
            int g_row = block_col + row;
            int g_col = k + col;
            __nv_bfloat16 val;
            if (g_row < N && g_col < K) {
                val = B[g_row * K + g_col];
            } else {
                val = __float2bfloat16(0.0f);
            }
            smem_B[row * BK + col] = val;
        }
        
        __syncthreads();
        
        for (int kk = 0; kk < BK; kk += 16) {
            load_matrix_sync(frag_a, &smem_A[warp_m * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            load_matrix_sync(frag_b, &smem_B[warp_n * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
            mma_sync(frag_c, frag_a, frag_b, frag_c);
        }
        
        __syncthreads();
    }
    
    {
        __shared__ float smem_float[BM * BN];
        store_matrix_sync(
            &smem_float[warp_m * 16 * BN + warp_n * 16],
            frag_c, BN, mem_row_major
        );
        __syncthreads();
        
        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BN; idx += THREADS) {
            int m = idx / BN;
            int n = idx % BN;
            int g_m = block_row + m;
            int g_n = block_col + n;
            if (g_m < M && g_n < N) {
                C[g_m * N + g_n] = __float2bfloat16(smem_float[m * BN + n]);
            }
        }
    }
}

extern \"C\" void launch_gemm(const void* A, const void* B, void* C, int M, int N, int K) {
    dim3 grid((M + BM - 1) / BM, (N + BN - 1) / BN);
    dim3 block(THREADS);
    fp8_gemm_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(
        static_cast<const __nv_fp8_e4m3*>(A),
        static_cast<const __nv_bfloat16*>(B),
        static_cast<__nv_bfloat16*>(C),
        M, N, K
    );
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
}
'''

mod = load_inline(

+"""FP8 e4m3 GEMM kernel using CUDA C++ with nvcuda::wmma (bf16 tensor cores).
+Converts fp8→bf16 on-the-fly during global→shared load, then uses bf16 WMMA.
+"""
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+
+# CUDA kernel source
+CUDA_SRC = r"""
+#include <cuda_runtime.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+#include <cuda_fp8.h>
+#include <mma.h>
+
+using namespace nvcuda::wmma;
+
+constexpr int BM = 32;
+constexpr int BN = 64;
+constexpr int BK = 32;
+constexpr int WARPS_M = BM / 16;
+constexpr int WARPS_N = BN / 16;
+constexpr int NUM_WARPS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N;
+constexpr int THREADS = NUM_WARPS * 32;
+
+__global__ void fp8_gemm_kernel(
+    const __nv_fp8_e4m3* __restrict__ A,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ B,
+    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ C,
+    int M, int N, int K
+) {
+    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_A[BM * BK];
+    __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_B[BN * BK];
+
+    int warp_id = threadIdx.x / 32;
+    int warp_m = warp_id % WARPS_M;
+    int warp_n = warp_id / WARPS_M;
+
+    int block_row = blockIdx.x * BM;
+    int block_col = blockIdx.y * BN;
+
+    fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> frag_a;
+    fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, col_major> frag_b;
+    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
+    fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);
+
+    for (int k = 0; k < K; k += BK) {
+        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BK; idx += THREADS) {
+            int row = idx / BK;
+            int col = idx % BK;
+            int g_row = block_row + row;
+            int g_col = k + col;
+            float fval;
+            if (g_row < M && g_col < K) {
+                fval = (float)A[g_row * K + g_col];
+            } else {
+                fval = 0.0f;
+            }
+            smem_A[row * BK + col] = __float2bfloat16(fval);
+        }
+
+        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BN * BK; idx += THREADS) {
+            int row = idx / BK;
+            int col = idx % BK;
+            int g_row = block_col + row;
+            int g_col = k + col;
+            __nv_bfloat16 val;
+            if (g_row < N && g_col < K) {
+                val = B[g_row * K + g_col];
+            } else {
+                val = __float2bfloat16(0.0f);
+            }
+            smem_B[row * BK + col] = val;
+        }
+
+        __syncthreads();
+
+        for (int kk = 0; kk < BK; kk += 16) {
+            load_matrix_sync(frag_a, &smem_A[warp_m * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
+            load_matrix_sync(frag_b, &smem_B[warp_n * 16 * BK + kk], BK);
+            mma_sync(frag_c, frag_a, frag_b, frag_c);
+        }
+
+        __syncthreads();
+    }
+
+    {
+        __shared__ float smem_float[BM * BN];
+        store_matrix_sync(
+            &smem_float[warp_m * 16 * BN + warp_n * 16],
+            frag_c, BN, mem_row_major
+        );
+        __syncthreads();
+
+        for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < BM * BN; idx += THREADS) {
+            int m = idx / BN;
+            int n = idx % BN;
+            int g_m = block_row + m;
+            int g_n = block_col + n;
+            if (g_m < M && g_n < N) {
+                C[g_m * N + g_n] = __float2bfloat16(smem_float[m * BN + n]);
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+extern "C" void launch_gemm(const void* A, const void* B, void* C, int M, int N, int K) {
+    dim3 grid((M + BM - 1) / BM, (N + BN - 1) / BN);
+    dim3 block(THREADS);
+    fp8_gemm_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(
+        static_cast<const __nv_fp8_e4m3*>(A),
+        static_cast<const __nv_bfloat16*>(B),
+        static_cast<__nv_bfloat16*>(C),
+        M, N, K
+    );
+    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
+}
+"""
+
+# Compile once at module load time
+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+
+_ext = load_inline(
+    name="fp8_gemm_sm120",
+    cpp_sources="void launch_gemm(const void* A, const void* B, void* C, int M, int N, int K);",
+    cuda_sources=CUDA_SRC,
+    extra_cuda_cflags=["-arch=sm_120", "-O3", "--expt-relaxed-constexpr"],
+    functions=["launch_gemm"],
+    verbose=False,
+)
+
+
+OP_TYPE = "gemm"
+SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["fp8_e4m3"]
+HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]
+
+
+class Model(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, M: int, N: int, K: int):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.M, self.N, self.K = M, N, K
+        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
+        nn.init.normal_(self.weight, std=0.02)
+
+    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        out = torch.empty(self.M, self.N, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=x.device)
+        _ext.launch_gemm(
+            x.data_ptr(),
+            self.weight.data_ptr(),
+            out.data_ptr(),
+            self.M, self.N, self.K,
+        )
+        return out
+
+
+M = 4096
+N = 4096
+K = 4096
+
+
+def get_inputs():
+    x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
+    return [x]
+
+
+def get_init_inputs():
+    return [M, N, K]

def check_correctness(
    reference_out: torch.Tensor,
    solution_out: torch.Tensor,
    dtype: torch.dtype | None = None,
    override: dict | None = None,
) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    """Return (passed, message). Integer comparisons are bitwise; floats use atol/rtol."""
    if reference_out.shape != solution_out.shape:
        return False, f"shape mismatch: ref={tuple(reference_out.shape)} sol={tuple(solution_out.shape)}"

    if torch.isnan(solution_out).any():
        return False, "solution contains NaN"
    if torch.isinf(solution_out).any():
        return False, "solution contains Inf"

    dtype = dtype or reference_out.dtype
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(dtype, override)

    if tol["atol"] == 0 and tol["rtol"] == 0:
        if torch.equal(reference_out, solution_out):
            return True, "ok (exact)"
        n_diff = (reference_out != solution_out).sum().item()
        return False, f"exact match required; {n_diff} elements differ"

    # Cast both to fp32 for the comparison to avoid dtype-specific allclose quirks
    ref_f = reference_out.float()
    sol_f = solution_out.float()

    if torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol["atol"], rtol=tol["rtol"]):
        return True, f"ok (atol={tol['atol']}, rtol={tol['rtol']})"

    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    allowed = tol["atol"] + tol["rtol"] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    max_diff = diff.max().item()
    max_rel = (diff / ref_f.abs().clamp_min(1e-30)).max().item()
    n_bad = int(bad.sum().item()

... (389 more chars)

stdout (1266 chars)
def tolerance_for_dtype(dtype: torch.dtype, override: dict | None = None) -> dict:
    """Lookup atol/rtol for a given dtype, with optional per-problem override.

    The override dict is keyed by str(dtype). Values may be:
      - a single number (or a string parseable as float, e.g. "5e-2") -> used
        as both atol and rtol
      - a dict {"atol": ..., "rtol": ...} -> used directly, with values coerced
    """
    # Accept several spellings of the same dtype key (PyYAML quirks):
    # "torch.bfloat16", "bfloat16", torch.bfloat16
    if override is not None:
        type_str = str(dtype)                  # "torch.bfloat16"
        short_str = type_str.split(".")[-1]    # "bfloat16"
        v = override.get(type_str, override.get(short_str))
        if v is not None:
            v = _coerce_float(v)
            if isinstance(v, (int, float)):
                return {"atol": float(v), "rtol": float(v)}
            if isinstance(v, dict):
                return {"atol": _coerce_float(v.get("atol", 0)),
                        "rtol": _coerce_float(v.get("rtol", 0))}
    if dtype not in DEFAULT_TOLERANCE:
        # Fall back to fp32 precision for unknown types.
        return DEFAULT_TOLERANCE[torch.float32]
    return DEFAULT_TOLERANCE[dtype]

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

# Test shape 1 (K=4127)
shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
print(f'Testing shape: {shape}')

reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)

    ok, msg = check_correctness(
        ref_out, sol_out,
        dtype=ref_out.dtype,
        override=tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case),
    )
    print(f'  {case.name}: {msg}')
    if not ok:
        # Debug

import torch

# Test how PyTorch converts fp8→bf16
x = torch.tensor([1.0, -16.625, -16.75, 0.5, -0.125], dtype=torch.float32)

# Check rounding

print('Any difference?', (x_bf16_pytorch != x_bf16_via_float).any())

tool
stdout (228 chars)
def tolerance_for_case(
    base: dict | None,
    case: NumericStressCase,
) -> dict | None:
    if case.tolerance is None:
        return base
    merged = dict(base or {})
    merged.update(case.tolerance)
    return merged

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]  # K=4127
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

x = base_inputs[0]  # fp8 input
w = ref_model.weight

# Check position (129, 519)
row, col = 129, 519
print(f'Position ({row}, {col}):')

# Compute x[row, :] in fp8 format
x_row_fp8 = x[row, :]
x_row_bf16 = x_row_fp8.to(torch.bfloat16)

# Compute w[col, :] (the relevant column of w^T = row of w)
w_col_bf16 = w[col, :]

# Manual dot product
ref_val = (x_row_bf16 * w_col_bf16).sum()
print(f'Reference: {ref_val} (bf16)')

# manual bf16 dot
dot_bf16 = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
for k in range(shape['K']):
    dot_bf16 += x_row_bf16[k] * w_col_bf16[k]
print(f'Manual bf16 dot: {dot_bf16}')

# f32 dot
dot_f32 = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for k in range(shape['K']):
    dot_f32 += x_row_bf16[k].float() * w_col_bf16[k].float()
print(f'Manual f32 dot: {dot_f32}')

# f32 -> bf16
print(f'f32->bf16: {dot_f32.to(torch.bfloat16)}')

# Block what my kernel computes:
# In my kernel, A_bf16[k] = __float2bfloat16((float)x_fp8[k])
# B_bf16[k] = w[col][k] (already bf16)
# MMA accumulates in f32
# Final: __float2bfloat16(accum_f32)
sol_val = sol_model(x)[row, col]
print(f'Solution: {sol_val}')

# chunked f32 accumulation (simulating my kernel's K tile loop)
accum = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
BK = 32
for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
    k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
    for k in range(k_start, k_end):
        # Match my kernel: fp8 -> float -> bf16 -> MMA (bf16*bf16 -> f32 accum)
        a_bf16 = x_row_fp8[k].to(torch.bfloat16)
        b_bf16 = w_col_bf16[k]
        # MMA would do bf16 * bf16 with f32 result
        accum += a_bf16.float() * b_bf16.float()
result_bf16 = accum.to(torch.bfloat16)
print(f'Chunked f32 accum -> bf16: {result_bf16}')

# Check the actual WMMA fragments for row 129, col 519
# row 129 is in block 4 (BM=32), warp 0 of block
# col 519 is in block 8 (BN=64), warp 0 of block (since 519/64=8, 519-8*64=7)

print(f'Block row: {row // 32} (block start: {row // 32 * 32})')
print(f'Block col: {col // 64} (block start: {col // 64 * 64})')
print(f'Warp row in block: {(row % 32) // 16}')
print(f'Warp col in block: {(col % 64) // 16}')
print(f'Warp offset: ((row % 32) // 16) * 4 + ((col % 64) // 16) = {((row % 32) // 16) * 4 + ((col % 64) // 16)}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness

reference.N = shape['N']

        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)

    override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    print(f'Case: {case.name}')
    print(f'  Override: {override}')
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    
    # Check what tolerance_for_dtype gives for bf16
    from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(torch.bfloat16, override)
    print(f'  Computed tolerance: {tol}')
    
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    if bad.any():
        print(f'  FAIL: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()} bad elements')
        max_diff = diff.max().item()
        max_idx = diff.argmax().item()
        print(f'  Max diff: {max_diff}')
        print(f'  Worst: ({max_idx // ref_out.shape[1]}, {max_idx % ref_out.shape[1]})')
        worst_row = max_idx // ref_out.shape[1]
        worst_col = max_idx % ref_out.shape[1]
        print(f'  ref={ref_out[worst_row, worst_col]}, sol={sol_out[worst_row, worst_col]}')
        print(f'  allowed={allowed[worst_row, worst_col]}')
    else:
        print(f'  PASS')
    print()

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype, check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)

    override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    
    print(f'Case: {case.name}, tolerance: {tol}')
    print(f'  bad: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()}, max_diff: {diff.max().item()}')
    
    if bad.any():
        # Show 5 worst
        excess = diff - allowed
        worst_indices = torch.topk(excess.flatten(), min(5, bad.sum().item())).indices
        for wi in worst_indices:
            r = wi.item() // ref_out.shape[1]
            c = wi.item() % ref_out.shape[1]
            print(f'  worst excess: ({r}, {c}) ref={ref_out[r,c]} sol={sol_out[r,c]} diff={diff[r,c]:.6f} allowed={allowed[r,c]:.6f}')
    print()

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

# Debug position (2583, 161)
r, c = 2583, 161
x = base_inputs[0]
w = ref_model.weight

# My kernel computes: accumulate over K tiles of BK=32
# The WMMA uses fragments of 16x16x16

# Compute the reference value
ref_val = (x[r,:].to(torch.bfloat16) * w[c,:]).sum()
print(f'Reference dot product: {ref_val}')

# Compute the manual bf16 dot (simulating WMMA)
BK = 32
accum = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
    k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
    for k in range(k_start, k_end):
        a_bf16 = x[r, k].to(torch.bfloat16)
        b_bf16 = w[c, k]
        accum += a_bf16.float() * b_bf16.float()
sol_val_via_f32 = accum.to(torch.bfloat16)
print(f'Manual f32 accum -> bf16: {sol_val_via_f32}')

# Check specific K tiles for large f32 intermediate values
accum_f32 = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
    k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
    partial = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for k in range(k_start, k_end):
        a_bf16 = x[r, k].to(torch.bfloat16)
        b_bf16 = w[c, k]
        partial += a_bf16.float() * b_bf16.float()
    accum_f32 += partial
    if k_start % 256 == 0 or partial.abs().item() > 1:
        print(f'  k={k_start}: partial={partial.item():.6f}, accum={accum_f32.item():.6f}')

print(f'Final f32 accum: {accum_f32.item():.6f}')
print(f'To bf16: {accum_f32.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# Now check the solution
sol_val = sol_model(x)[r, c]
print(f'Solution: {sol_val.item():.6f}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    r, c = 1778, 3348
    
    x_fp8 = inputs[0]
    w = ref_model.weight  # bf16 weight
    
    x_bf16 = x_fp8.to(torch.bfloat16)
    ref_val = (x_bf16[r,:] * w[c,:]).sum()
    print(f'Position ({r}, {c})')
    print(f'  Reference: {ref_out[r,c]}')
    print(f'  Solution: {sol_out[r,c]}')
    print(f'  Manual ref (dot product): {ref_val}')
    
    # Check this specific dot product
    x_row = x_bf16[r, :]
    w_row = w[c, :]
    
    # Find what contributes the most
    contrib = (x_row * w_row).float()
    sort_idx = torch.argsort(contrib.abs(), descending=True)
    
    print(f'  Top 5 contributions:')
    for idx in sort_idx[:5]:
        print(f'    k={idx.item()}: x={x_fp8[r, idx].to(torch.bfloat16).item()}, w={w[c, idx].item()}, contrib={contrib[idx].item():.6f}')
    
    # Check the dot product computed with fp8 precision
    # My kernel does: fp8 -> float -> bf16 -> then bf16 * bf16 with f32 accum
    # Reference does: fp8 -> bf16 -> then bf16 * bf16 with f32 accum (via cuBLAS)
    
    # Try reproducing with my kernel's approach
    BK = 32
    accum_f32 = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
        k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
        partial = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
        for k in range(k_start, k_end):
            a_bf16 = x_fp8[r, k].to(torch.bfloat16)
            b_bf16 = w[c, k]
            partial += a_bf16.float() * b_bf16.float()
        accum_f32 += partial
    print(f'  Kernel-style dot: {accum_f32.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

import torch

# Test all possible fp8_e4m3 values
print('Testing ALL fp8_e4m3 values...')

all_match = True
for i in range(256):
    val = torch.tensor(i, dtype=torch.uint8).view(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
    
    # Path 1: PyTorch's conversion
    bf16_pytorch = val.to(torch.bfloat16)
    
    # Path 2: float then bf16 (what my kernel does)
    float_val = val.float()
    bf16_via_float = float_val.to(torch.bfloat16)
    
    if bf16_pytorch != bf16_via_float:
        print(f'Mismatch: fp8_hex={i:02x} fp8={val} -> pytorch={bf16_pytorch} vs float_path={bf16_via_float}')
        all_match = False

if all_match:
    print('All 256 fp8_e4m3 values match!')
else:
    print('Some values differ!')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None
print('tol_override:', tol_override)

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    print('Case large_input override:', override)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
    print('Computed tolerance:', tol)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    
    # Check worst position
    r, c = 0, 1501
    print(f'Position ({r}, {c}):')
    print(f'  ref={ref_out[r,c]}, sol={sol_out[r,c]}')
    print(f'  diff={diff[r,c]:.6f}, allowed={allowed[r,c]:.6f}')
    
    # Find all bad positions and check their reference values
    print(f'Number of bad elements: {bad.sum().item()}')
    
    # Show top 10 by excess
    excess = diff - allowed
    worst_values = torch.topk(excess.flatten(), min(10, bad.sum().item()))
    print('Top 10 worst by excess:')
    for idx, val in zip(worst_values.indices, worst_values.values):
        r = idx.item() // ref_out.shape[1]
        c = idx.item() % ref_out.shape[1]
        print(f'  ({r}, {c}): ref={ref_out[r,c].item():.6f}, sol={sol_out[r,c].item():.6f}, diff={diff[r,c].item():.6f}, allowed={allowed[r,c].item():.6f}')

stdout (534 chars)
@contextmanager
def numeric_stress_context(
    ref_model: torch.nn.Module,
    sol_model: torch.nn.Module,
    inputs: Sequence[object],
    case: NumericStressCase,
) -> Iterator[list[object]]:
    backups = _scale_states([ref_model, sol_model], case.state_scales)
    try:
        yield _scale_inputs(inputs, case.input_scales)
    finally:
        if torch.cuda.is_available():
            torch.cuda.synchronize()
        with torch.no_grad():
            for tensor, original in backups:
                tensor.copy_(original)

def numeric_stress_cases(problem_name: str) -> tuple[NumericStressCase, ...]:
    if os.environ.get("KBH_NUMERIC_STRESS", "1").lower() in {"0", "false", "no"}:
        return (NOMINAL_CASE,)
    return (NOMINAL_CASE, *_CASES.get(problem_name, ()))

tool
stdout (488 chars)
def _scale_inputs(inputs: Sequence[object], scales: Mapping[int, float]) -> list[object]:
    out = list(inputs)
    for idx, scale in scales.items():
        if idx >= len(out):
            raise IndexError(f"input scale index {idx} out of range for {len(out)} inputs")
        value = out[idx]
        if not isinstance(value, torch.Tensor):
            raise TypeError(f"input {idx} is not a tensor and cannot be scaled")
        out[idx] = _scale_tensor(value, scale)
    return out

tool
stdout (279 chars)
def _scale_tensor(tensor: torch.Tensor, scale: float) -> torch.Tensor:
    if not torch.is_floating_point(tensor):
        raise TypeError(f"cannot scale non-floating tensor dtype={tensor.dtype}")
    return (tensor.float() * scale).to(dtype=tensor.dtype, device=tensor.device)

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.numeric_stress import _scale_tensor
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

# Manually replicate the large_input stress case
x = base_inputs[0]  # fp8
w = ref_model.weight  # bf16

# large_input: scale input 0 by 64
x_scaled = _scale_tensor(x, 64.0)
print(f'x range: [{x.min().float().item():.3f}, {x.max().float().item():.3f}]')
print(f'x_scaled range: [{x_scaled.min().float().item():.3f}, {x_scaled.max().float().item():.3f}]')

# Check position (525, 2711)
r, c = 525, 2711

# Reference: x_scaled (fp8) -> bf16
x_bf16 = x_scaled.to(torch.bfloat16)
w_bf16 = w  # already bf16

# Reference dot product
ref_val = (x_bf16[r,:] * w_bf16[c,:]).float().sum()
print(f'Reference: {ref_val.item():.6f}')
print(f'Reference (to bf16): {ref_val.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# My kernel's approach: fp8 -> float -> bf16 (same as x_bf16 since they match)
# Then bf16 * bf16 -> f32 accum

# Check if reference and my kernel would use the same conv
a_bf16 = x_scaled[r, :].to(torch.bfloat16)
b_bf16 = w_bf16[c, :]

# Simulate my kernel: tile K in BK=32, sub-tile in 16
BK = 32
accum = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
    k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
    partial = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for k in range(k_start, k_end):
        partial += a_bf16[k].float() * b_bf16[k].float()
    accum += partial
print(f'Kernel-style f32 accum: {accum.item():.6f} -> bf16: {accum.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# Now check the actual solution output
sol_out = sol_model(x_scaled.unsqueeze(0))[0]  # forward takes (1, M, K)? No, forward takes (M, K)
print(f'Solution: {sol_out[r,c].item():.6f}')

# Check a few more elements
print()
print(f'Expected output (reference matmul):')
ref_out = x_bf16 @ w_bf16.T
print(f'  ref[{r},{c}] = {ref_out[r,c].item():.6f}')
print(f'  sol[{r},{c}] = {sol_out[r,c].item():.6f}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path
import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype, check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

for seed in (42, 123, 456):
    torch.manual_seed(seed)
    torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
    base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]
    
    for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
        with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
            with torch.no_grad():
                ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
                sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
        
        override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
        tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
        ok, msg = check_correctness(ref_out, sol_out, dtype=ref_out.dtype, override=override)
        
        if not ok:
            ref_f = ref_out.float()
            sol_f = sol_out.float()
            diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
            allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
            bad = diff > allowed
            
            print(f'Seed {seed}, case {case.name}: FAIL')
            print(f'  bad: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()}, max_diff: {diff.max().item():.6f}')
            
            excess = diff - allowed
            sorted_idx = torch.argsort(excess.flatten(), descending=True)
            for i in range(5):
                idx = sorted_idx[i].item()
                r = idx // ref_out.shape[1]
                c = idx % ref_out.shape[1]
                print(f'  worst {i}: ({r}, {c}) ref={ref_out[r,c].item():.6f} sol={sol_out[r,c].item():.6f} diff={diff[r,c].item():.6f} allowed={allowed[r,c].item():.6f}')
            print()

1: """FP8 e4m3 GEMM kernel using CUDA C++ with nvcuda::wmma (bf16 tensor cores).
2: Converts fp8→bf16 on-the-fly during global→shared load, then uses bf16 WMMA.
3: """
4: import torch
5: import torch.nn as nn
6: 
7: # CUDA kernel source
8: CUDA_SRC = r"""
9: #include <cuda_runtime.h>
10: #include <cuda_bf16.h>
11: #include <cuda_fp8.h>
12: #include <mma.h>
13: 
14: using namespace nvcuda::wmma;
15: 
16: constexpr int BM = 32;
17: constexpr int BN = 64;
18: constexpr int BK = 32;
19: constexpr int WARPS_M = BM / 16;
20: constexpr int WARPS_N = BN / 16;
21: constexpr int NUM_WARPS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N;
22: constexpr int THREADS = NUM_WARPS * 32;
23: 
24: __global__ void fp8_gemm_kernel(
25:     const __nv_fp8_e4m3* __restrict__ A,
26:     const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ B,
27:     __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ C,
28:     int M, int N, int K
29: ) {
30:     __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_A[BM * BK];
31:     __shared__ __nv_bfloat16 smem_B[BN * BK];
32: 
33:     int warp_id = threadIdx.x / 32;
34:     int warp_m = warp_id % WARPS_M;
35:     int warp_n = warp_id / WARPS_M;
36: 
37:     int block_row = blockIdx.x * BM;
38:     int block_col = blockIdx.y * BN;
39: 
40:     fragment<matrix_a, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, row_major> frag_a;
41:     fragment<matrix_b, 16, 16, 16, __nv_bfloat16, col_major> frag_b;
42:     fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
43:     fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (
    numeric_stress_cases,
    numeric_stress_context,
    tolerance_for_case,
)
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness, tolerance_for_dtype

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]

reference.M = shape['M']
reference.N = shape['N']
reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

seed = 42
torch.manual_seed(seed)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    print('override:', override)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
    print('tol:', tol)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    
    print(f'Bad elements: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()}')
    print(f'Max diff: {diff.max().item()}')
    print(f'Max allowed at worst: {allowed[diff.argmax()].item() if diff.numel() > 0 else 0}')
    
    # Check a specific bad element
    excess = diff - allowed
    worst_excess = torch.argmax(excess.flatten()).item()
    wr = worst_excess // ref_out.shape[1]
    wc = worst_excess % ref_out.shape[1]
    print(f'Worst excess: ({wr}, {wc})')
    print(f'  ref = {ref_out[wr, wc].item()}')
    print(f'  sol = {sol_out[wr, wc].item()}')
    print(f'  diff = {diff[wr, wc].item()}')
    print(f'  allowed = {allowed[wr, wc].item()}')
    print(f'  excess = {excess[wr, wc].item()}')
    
    # Show a few more bad elements
    sorted_excess = torch.argsort(excess.flatten(), descending=True)
    print('Top 5 by excess:')
    for i in range(5):
        idx = sorted_excess[i].item()
        r = idx // ref_out.shape[1]
        c = idx % ref_out.shape[1]
        print(f'  ({r}, {c}): ref={ref_out[r,c].item()} sol={sol_out[r,c].item()} diff={diff[r,c].item()} allowed={allowed[r,c].item()}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

# Test all shapes for large_input case
for shape_idx, shape in enumerate(shapes.SHAPES):
    reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']
    
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sd = ref_model.state_dict()
    sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)
    
    for seed in (42, 123, 456):
        torch.manual_seed(seed)
        torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
        base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]
        
        for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
            if case.name == 'nominal':
                continue  # skip nominal, we know it passes with the right tolerance
            
            with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
                with torch.no_grad():
                    ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
                    sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
            
            ok, msg = check_correctness(
                ref_out, sol_out,
                dtype=ref_out.dtype,
                override=tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case),
            )
            status = 'OK' if ok else 'FAIL'
            print(f'Shape {shape_idx} seed {seed} case {case.name}: {status}  ({msg[:50]})')

" 2>&1
tool
stdout (855 chars)
def _scale_states(
    models: Sequence[torch.nn.Module],
    scales: Mapping[str, float],
) -> list[tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]]:
    backups: list[tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]] = []
    if not scales:
        return backups
    for model in models:
        state = dict(model.named_parameters())
        state.update(dict(model.named_buffers()))
        for name, scale in scales.items():
            if name not in state:
                raise KeyError(f"state scale target {name!r} not found")
            tensor = state[name]
            if not torch.is_floating_point(tensor):
                raise TypeError(f"state scale target {name!r} is not floating point")
            backups.append((tensor, tensor.detach().clone()))
            with torch.no_grad():
                tensor.copy_(_scale_tensor(tensor, scale))
    return backups

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

# Get outputs for two runs with same input
for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        x_in = inputs[0].clone()
    
    # Run twice
    out1 = sol_model(x_in)
    out2 = sol_model(x_in)
    
    diff = (out1 - out2).abs().max().item()
    print(f'Determinism check: max diff between two runs = {diff}')
    print(f'  Deterministic: {diff == 0}')

    # Compare with reference

    x_bf16 = x_in.to(torch.bfloat16)
    ref = x_bf16 @ w.T
    
    sol_diff = (out1 - ref).abs().max().item()
    print(f'Max diff vs reference: {sol_diff}')
    
    # Check specific bad positions

    sol_f = out1.float()
    diff_t = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    
    # Find elements where reference is tiny but solution is ~1.0
    mask_small_ref = ref_f.abs() < 1.0
    mask_large_diff = diff_t > 0.5
    combined = mask_small_ref & mask_large_diff
    n_bad = combined.sum().item()
    print(f'Elements with |ref|<1 and diff>0.5: {n_bad}')
    
    if n_bad > 0:
        # Show some
        bad_indices = torch.nonzero(combined)
        for i in range(min(5, len(bad_indices))):
            r, c = bad_indices[i].tolist()
            print(f'  ({r}, {c}): ref={ref[r,c].item():.6f} sol={out1[r,c].item():.6f}')

    x_bf16 = x_in.to(torch.bfloat16)

    # Check specific position
    r, c = 3054, 2940
    
    # Row 3054 is in block: block_row = 3054 // 32 = 95, offset = 3054 % 32 = 14
    # Warp_row in block = 14 // 16 = 0 (within the first 16 rows of the block)
    # Wait, 14 < 16, so warp_m = 0. But there are WARPS_M=2 warps per block.
    # Warp 0 handles rows 0-15, warp 1 handles rows 16-31.
    # So row 14 is in warp 0.
    
    block_row = r // 32 * 32
    warp_m = (r % 32) // 16
    row_in_warp = (r % 32) % 16
    
    print(f'Row {r}: block_row={block_row}, warp_m={warp_m}, row_in_warp={row_in_warp}')
    
    # Column 2940 is in block: block_col = 2940 // 64 = 45, offset = 2940 % 64 = 60
    # Warp_n in block = 60 // 16 = 3 (within the 4th 16-column group)
    
    block_col = c // 64 * 64
    warp_n = (c % 64) // 16
    col_in_warp = (c % 64) % 16
    
    print(f'Col {c}: block_col={block_col}, warp_n={warp_n}, col_in_warp={col_in_warp}')
    
    # Compute manually: C[m][n] = sum_k A[m][k] * B[n][k]
    # For this element: C[3054][2940] = sum_k A[3054][k] * B[2940][k]
    
    # My kernel computes this as:
    # warp_m=0, warp_n=3 in the block
    # The warp handles 16x16 output: rows [block_row, block_row+15], cols [block_col+n*16, block_col+n*16+15]
    # = [3040, 3055] × [2944, 2959]
    
    # Wait, block_col = 45 * 64 = 2880. So cols [2880, 2943].
    # Column 2940 is at offset 60 within the block, which is in warp_n = 60//16 = 3, at col_in_warp = 60%16 = 12.
    
    # But my kernel's warp_n ranges from 0 to WARPS_N-1 = 0..3
    # Wait, there are WARPS_N = BN/16 = 64/16 = 4 warps in the N direction.
    # Warp 0: cols [0,15], Warp 1: cols [16,31], Warp 2: cols [32,47], Warp 3: cols [48,63]
    
    # So column 2940 has block offset 2940-2880=60, which is in warp 3 (offset 48-63).
    # col_in_warp = 60-48 = 12.
    
    print(f'  block_col={block_col}, block_offset={c - block_col}')
    print(f'  warp_n={warp_n}, col_in_warp={col_in_warp}')
    
    # Now let's compute the partial sums per K tile
    BK = 32
    K = shape['K']
    
    accum_kernel = 0.0
    accum_ref_f32 = 0.0
    
    for k_start in range(0, K, BK):
        k_end = min(k_start + BK, K)
        
        # My kernel's approach: fp8 -> float -> bf16 -> then WMMA bf16*bf16 -> f32 accum
        partial_kernel = 0.0
        partial_ref = 0.0
        
        for k in range(k_start, k_end):
            a_bf16 = x_in[r, k].to(torch.bfloat16).float().item()
            b_bf16 = w[c, k].float().item()
            
            # My kernel: bf16 * bf16 -> f32 product
            # This is what WMMA does internally
            partial_kernel += a_bf16 * b_bf16
        
        accum_kernel += partial_kernel
        
        # The reference does the same bf16 matmul via cuBLAS
        # which also accumulates in f32
        # But the tiling might be different
    
    # Ref

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

# Test fill_fragment correctness
cuda_src = '''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cuda_bf16.h>
#include <mma.h>

using namespace nvcuda::wmma;

__global__ void test_fill() {
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_c;
    fill_fragment(frag_c, 0.0f);
    
    // Check all elements are 0
    bool all_zero = true;
    for (int i = 0; i < frag_c.num_elements; i++) {
        if (frag_c.x[i] != 0.0f) {
            all_zero = false;
        }
    }
    
    // Also test with init
    fragment<accumulator, 16, 16, 16, float> frag_d;
    fill_fragment(frag_d, 1.0f);
}

extern \"C\" int test_fill_fragment() {
    test_fill<<<1, 256>>>();
    cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    return cudaPeekAtLastError();
}
'''

mod = load_inline(
    name='test_fill',
    cpp_sources='int test_fill_fragment();',
    cuda_sources=cuda_src,
    extra_cuda_cflags=['-arch=sm_120', '-O3', '--expt-relaxed-constexpr'],
    functions=['test_fill_fragment'],
    verbose=False,
)

result = mod.test_fill_fragment()
print(f'Result: {result}')
print('fill_fragment test passed!')

# Test shape 1 with pure f32 matmul

# So even f32 matmul -> bf16 gives different results from bf16 matmul
# This is because bf16 matmul uses tensor cores with f32 accum internally
# while f32 matmul uses CUDA cores with f32 arithmetic throughout

# Question: does bf16 matmul (cuBLAS on SM120) give the SAME result
# as WMMA bf16 matmul? Let's test with a small case.

# cuBLAS bf16 matmul
ref_bf16_2 = x2_bf16 @ w2.T

# f32 matmul
ref_f32_2 = x2_bf16.float() @ w2.float().T
ref_f32_to_bf16_2 = ref_f32_2.to(torch.bfloat16)

diff2 = (ref_bf16_2 - ref_f32_to_bf16_2).abs()
print(f'bf16 matmul vs f32->bf16: mean={diff2.mean().item():.6f} max={diff2.max().item():.6f}')
print(f'  Identical: {(diff2 == 0).all().item()}')

import torch

# Test fp8 quantization effect on dot products
torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)

K = 4127
x_float = torch.rand(1, K, device='cuda') * 8 - 4  # [-4, 4]
w = torch.randn(1, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')

# fp8 quantize x
x_fp8 = x_float.to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
x_bf16 = x_fp8.to(torch.bfloat16)

# Reference dot product (bf16 @ bf16 -> f32 -> bf16)
ref = (x_bf16 * w).float().sum().to(torch.bfloat16)
print(f'Reference (bf16 matmul-like): {ref.item():.6f}')

# Now simulate what WMMA does: bf16 * bf16 -> f32 accum, then bf16 output
# The WMMA does this for 16x16 tiles at a time
# Let's accumulate in f32
accum_f32 = 0.0
for k in range(K):
    a_bf16 = x_bf16[0, k].float().item()
    b_bf16 = w[0, k].float().item()
    accum_f32 += a_bf16 * b_bf16

accum_bf16 = torch.tensor(accum_f32, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
print(f'f32 accum -> bf16: {accum_bf16.item():.6f}')

# cuBLAS bf16 matmul
ref_matmul = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[0, 0]
print(f'cuBLAS bf16 matmul: {ref_matmul.item():.6f}')

# Now try the same with scaled input (large_input simulation)
scale = 64.0
x_scaled_float = x_float * scale
x_scaled_fp8 = x_scaled_float.to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
x_scaled_bf16 = x_scaled_fp8.to(torch.bfloat16)

ref_scaled = (x_scaled_bf16 * w).float().sum().to(torch.bfloat16)
print(f'')
print(f'With scale={scale}:')
print(f'Reference (sum bf16->bf16): {ref_scaled.item():.6f}')

# cuBLAS bf16 matmul with scaled input
ref_scaled_matmul = (x_scaled_bf16 @ w.T)[0, 0]
print(f'cuBLAS bf16 matmul: {ref_scaled_matmul.item():.6f}')

# f32 accum
accum_scaled_f32 = 0.0
for k in range(K):
    a_bf16 = x_scaled_bf16[0, k].float().item()
    b_bf16 = w[0, k].float().item()
    accum_scaled_f32 += a_bf16 * b_bf16
accum_scaled_bf16 = torch.tensor(accum_scaled_f32, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
print(f'f32 accum -> bf16: {accum_scaled_bf16.item():.6f}')

    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        x_in = inputs[0].clone()
    
    # Check a specific bad position
    r, c = 3054, 2940
    
    x_bf16 = x_in.to(torch.bfloat16)
    w = sol_model.weight
    
    # Compute dot product in different ways
    # 1. cuBLAS bf16 matmul
    ref_cublas = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[r, c]
    
    # 2. Manual f32 accumulate (all elements)
    accum_f32 = 0.0
    for k in range(shape['K']):
        accum_f32 += x_bf16[r, k].float().item() * w[c, k].float().item()
    accum_bf16 = torch.tensor(accum_f32, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
    
    # 3. My kernel
    sol_val = sol_model(x_in)[r, c]
    
    print(f'cuBLAS:  {ref_cublas.item():.6f}')
    print(f'f32 accum -> bf16: {accum_bf16.item():.6f}')
    print(f'f32 accum (raw): {accum_f32:.10f}')
    print(f'Sol:     {sol_val.item():.6f}')
    
    # Check if this is even in the same range
    print(f'x[r,:] range: [{x_in[r,:].float().min().item():.3f}, {x_in[r,:].float().max().item():.3f}]')
    print(f'w[c,:] range: [{w[c,:].float().min().item():.6f}, {w[c,:].float().max().item():.6f}]')
    
    # Check the partial sums
    BK = 32
    print(f'\\nPartial sums (per K tile of {BK}):')
    for k_start in range(0, shape['K'], BK):
        k_end = min(k_start + BK, shape['K'])
        partial = 0.0
        for k in range(k_start, k_end):
            partial += x_bf16[r, k].float().item() * w[c, k].float().item()
        print(f'  k={k_start:4d}: partial={partial:.6f}, valid={k_end-k_start}')

        accum_f32 += x_bf16[r, k].float().item() * w[c, k].float().item()

from pathlib import Path
import torch
import yaml

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (
    numeric_stress_cases,
    numeric_stress_context,
    tolerance_for_case,
)

import reference, shapes, solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

# Only test shape 1, seed 42, case large_input

reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()

sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

seed = 42
torch.manual_seed(seed)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    ok, msg = check_correctness(
        ref_out, sol_out,
        dtype=ref_out.dtype,
        override=tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case),
    )
    print(f'Result: {msg}')
    
    if not ok:
        ref_f = ref_out.float()
        sol_f = sol_out.float()
        diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
        
        # Find bad elements
        override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
        from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype
        tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
        allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
        bad = diff > allowed
        
        # Show first bad element
        bad_indices = torch.nonzero(bad)
        print(f'Total bad: {bad.sum().item()}')
        
        # Verify by checking the models directly
        x_in = inputs[0].clone()
        
        # Now call sol_model directly (should use same weights)
        sol_out2 = sol_model(x_in)
        diff2 = (sol_out2 - ref_out).float().abs()
        bad2 = diff2 > allowed
        print(f'Bad after direct call: {bad2.sum().item()}')
        
        # The stress context restores model state after exit
        # But we captured x_in inside the context, and called sol_model outside
        # If weight was modified by context and restored, the results should match
        
        # Actually the issue might be that 'inputs' changes after context exits
        # since _scale_tensor creates a new tensor
        print(f'x_in same as inside? {torch.equal(x_in, inputs[0]) if len(inputs) > 0 else \"N/A\"}')
        print(f'Weight same inside/outside: {torch.equal(sol_model.weight, ref_model.weight)}')

import torch, sys
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

# Compare K=4096 vs K=4127
M, N = 4096, 4096

for K in [4096, 4127]:
    torch.manual_seed(42)
    x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()
    w = torch.randn(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16).cuda()
    
    x_scaled = (x.float() * 64.0).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)
    
    import solution
    model = solution.Model(M, N, K).cuda()
    model.weight.data.copy_(w)
    
    x_bf16 = x_scaled.to(torch.bfloat16)
    ref = x_bf16 @ w.T
    out = model(x_scaled)
    
    diff = (out - ref).abs()
    print(f'K={K}: max_diff={diff.max().item():.4f} mean_diff={diff.mean().item():.6f}')
    
    # Check specific elements near zero
    small_ref = ref.float().abs() < 1.0
    large_diff = diff > 0.5
    bad = small_ref & large_diff
    print(f'  |ref|<1 & diff>0.5: {bad.sum().item()}')
    
    # Show worst
    max_idx = diff.argmax().item()
    r = max_idx // N
    c = max_idx % N
    print(f'  worst: ({r}, {c}) ref={ref[r,c].item():.4f} sol={out[r,c].item():.4f} diff={diff[r,c].item():.4f}')
    print()

    print()

import torch, sys
from pathlib import Path

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()
w = torch.randn(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16).cuda()
x_scaled = (x.float() * 64.0).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)

# Test position (1, 2529)
r, c = 1, 2529

a_bf16 = x_bf16[r, :]  # bf16
b_bf16 = w[c, :]  # bf16

# Method 1: element-wise float product, float sum
dot_f32 = (a_bf16.float() * b_bf16.float()).sum()
print(f'f32 dot: {dot_f32.item():.10f}')
print(f'f32 dot -> bf16: {dot_f32.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# Method 2: bf16 matmul via torch
ref = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[r, c]
print(f'bf16 matmul (cuBLAS): {ref.item():.6f}')

# Method 3: bf16 matmul with specific options
ref2 = torch.matmul(x_bf16[r:r+1, :], w[c:c+1, :].T)[0, 0]
print(f'bf16 matmul (single row/col): {ref2.item():.6f}')

# Method 4: explicit f32 accumulation (per K tile)
BK = 32
accum = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for k_start in range(0, K, BK):
    k_end = min(k_start + BK, K)
    a_tile = a_bf16[k_start:k_end].float()
    b_tile = b_bf16[k_start:k_end].float()
    accum += (a_tile * b_tile).sum()
print(f'f32 accum per-tile: {accum.item():.10f}')
print(f'f32 accum per-tile -> bf16: {accum.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# Method 5: check if different col-major layout matters
# Try the bf16 matmul with explicit col-major B
# Actually, w is already (N, K) and w.T is (K, N)

# 5. Single row, all columns

methods['1 row, full cols'] = ref_single_row[0, c].item()

import torch, sys
from pathlib import Path

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()

x_scaled = (x.float() * 64.0).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)

print(f'w.T.is_contiguous(): {w.T.is_contiguous()}')
print(f'w.T.contiguous().is_contiguous(): {w.T.contiguous().is_contiguous()}')

print(f'x @ w.T: {ref1[r, c].item():.6f}')

ref2 = x_bf16 @ w_T_contig
print(f'x @ w.T.contiguous(): {ref2[r, c].item():.6f}')

# With explicit transposition
# x_bf16 @ w.T = (w @ x_bf16.T).T
ref3 = (w @ x_bf16.T).T
print(f'(w @ x.T).T: {ref3[r, c].item():.6f}')

ref4 = x_bf16[r:r+1, :] @ w[c:c+1, :].T
print(f'Single row/col: {ref4[0, 0].item():.6f}')

# Single element with contiguous
ref5 = x_bf16[r:r+1, :] @ w[c:c+1, :].T.contiguous()
print(f'Single row/col (contiguous B^T): {ref5[0, 0].item():.6f}')

import torch, sys
from pathlib import Path

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()

# Try different matmul approaches
# 1. Original: x @ w.T
v1 = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[r, c]

# 2. With w transposed and contiguous
w_T = w.T.contiguous()  # explicit transpose, contiguous (K, N)
v2 = (x_bf16 @ w_T)[r, c]

# 3. Using torch.bmm or torch.addmm
v3 = torch.addmm(torch.zeros(1, device=device), x_bf16[r:r+1], w_T[c:c+1].T)[0, 0]

# 4. Using torch.mm instead of @
v4 = torch.mm(x_bf16, w.T)[r, c]

# 5. Using matmul instead of @
v5 = torch.matmul(x_bf16, w.T)[r, c]

print(f'x_bf16 @ w.T: {v1.item():.6f}')
print(f'x @ w_T (contiguous): {v2.item():.6f}')
print(f'addmm: {v3.item():.6f}')
print(f'mm: {v4.item():.6f}')
print(f'matmul: {v5.item():.6f}')

# Check the f32 reference
x_f32 = x_bf16.float()
w_f32 = w.float()
v_f32 = (x_f32 @ w_f32.T)[r, c]
print(f'f32: {v_f32.item():.6f} -> bf16: {v_f32.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

print()

print('Any discrepancy indicates a cuBLAS precision issue')

    print(f'torch.compile: {v_compiled.item():.6f}')
except:
    print('torch.compile failed')

import torch, sys
from pathlib import Path

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()
w = torch.randn(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16).cuda()
x_scaled = (x.float() * 64.0).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)

x_bf16 = x_scaled.to(torch.bfloat16)
x_f32 = x_bf16.float()
w_f32 = w.float()

r, c = 1, 2529

# f32 matmul as ground truth
v_f32 = (x_f32 @ w_f32.T)[r, c]
print(f'f32 ground truth: {v_f32.item():.10f} -> bf16: {v_f32.to(torch.bfloat16).item():.6f}')

# bf16 matmul variants  
v1 = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[r, c]
print(f'x @ w.T: {v1.item():.6f}')

# Explicitly make w contiguous and transposed properly
# w is (N, K) row-major. w.T is (K, N) column-major (non-contiguous)
# w_T_contig makes it (K, N) row-major contiguous
w_T_contig = w.T.contiguous()  # Now (K, N) row-major
v2 = (x_bf16 @ w_T_contig)[r, c]
print(f'x @ w.T (contiguous): {v2.item():.6f}')

# Try the matrix mult the other way: (w @ x.T).T
v3 = (w @ x_bf16.T).T
print(f'(w @ x.T).T: {v3[r, c].item():.6f}')

# With contiguous version
w_contig = w.contiguous()  # Already contiguous
v4 = (w_contig @ x_bf16.T).T
print(f'(w_contig @ x.T).T: {v4[r, c].item():.6f}')

# Just compare all rows of the result
print()
print('Comparing row 1 of bf16 matmul with f32 matmul:')
row_bf16 = (x_bf16 @ w.T)[1, :]
row_f32 = (x_f32 @ w_f32.T)[1, :].to(torch.bfloat16)
diff = (row_bf16 - row_f32).abs()
print(f'  max diff: {diff.max().item():.6f}')
print(f'  mean diff: {diff.mean().item():.6f}')

# Check specifically where differences are large
large = diff > 1.0
print(f'  elements with diff>1: {large.sum().item()}')
if large.any():
    bad_indices = torch.nonzero(large)[:5]
    for i in range(len(bad_indices)):
        ci = bad_indices[i].item()
        print(f'  col {ci}: bf16={row_bf16[ci].item():.6f} f32->bf16={row_f32[ci].item():.6f}')

import torch, sys
from pathlib import Path

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x_fp8 = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()

# Try with different matmul precision settings
# By default, PyTorch uses the highest precision available
# Let's try forcing fp32 accumulation
with torch.backends.cuda.matmul.allow_fp32_reduced_precision_reduction(False):
    pass  # This doesn't help with bf16

# Actually, let me check the cuBLAS workspace config
torch.backends.cuda.matmul.allow_tf32 = True
print(f'allow_tf32: {torch.backends.cuda.matmul.allow_tf32}')

# The issue might be related to how cuBLAS handles K=4127 (= 4127 = 31 mod 32 = 31 mod 128)
# Let me try using the Fp8Matmul specialization
# torch._scaled_mm is forbidden, but let's check if there's another way

# Actually, wait. Let me check the bf16 matmul output more carefully
# Maybe the issue is with how I'm measuring it

ref2 = (x_bf16.float() @ w.float().T).to(torch.bfloat16)

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[1]
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    merged = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, merged)
    print(f'tol: {tol}')
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    
    print(f'Bad: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()}')
    print(f'Max diff: {diff.max().item()}')
    
    # Check worst position
    worst_flat = diff.argmax().item()
    wr = worst_flat // ref_out.shape[1]
    wc = worst_flat % ref_out.shape[1]
    print(f'Worst (by diff): ({wr}, {wc}) ref={ref_out[wr,wc].item():.6f} sol={sol_out[wr,wc].item():.6f}')
    
    # Find worst by excess
    excess = diff - allowed
    worst_excess = torch.topk(excess.flatten(), 5)
    for i, idx in enumerate(worst_excess.indices):
        r = idx.item() // ref_out.shape[1]
        c = idx.item() % ref_out.shape[1]
        print(f'  worst excess {i}: ({r}, {c}) ref={ref_out[r,c].item():.6f} sol={sol_out[r,c].item():.6f} diff={diff[r,c].item():.6f} allowed={allowed[r,c].item():.6f}')

import torch

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()
w = torch.randn(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16).cuda()
w_fp8 = w.to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)

# fp8 to bf16 references
x_bf16 = x.to(torch.bfloat16)
w_bf16 = w

# Regular bf16 matmul (cuBLAS)
ref_bf16 = x_bf16 @ w_bf16.T

# f32 matmul (ground truth)
ref_f32 = (x_bf16.float() @ w_bf16.float().T).to(torch.bfloat16)

# torch._scaled_mm (fp8 tensor cores)
scale_a = torch.tensor(1.0, device=device)
scale_b = torch.tensor(1.0, device=device)
try:
    result = torch._scaled_mm(x, w_fp8.T, scale_a=scale_a, scale_b=scale_b, out_dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    ref_fp8 = result if not isinstance(result, tuple) else result[0]
    
    diff_fp8_vs_f32 = (ref_fp8 - ref_f32).abs().max().item()
    diff_fp8_vs_bf16 = (ref_fp8 - ref_bf16).abs().max().item()
    diff_bf16_vs_f32 = (ref_bf16 - ref_f32).abs().max().item()
    
    print(f'torch._scaled_mm vs f32: max_diff = {diff_fp8_vs_f32:.4f}')
    print(f'torch._scaled_mm vs bf16 (cuBLAS): max_diff = {diff_fp8_vs_bf16:.4f}')
    print(f'bf16 (cuBLAS) vs f32: max_diff = {diff_bf16_vs_f32:.4f}')
    
    # Check a specific element
    r, c = 1, 2529
    print(f'Element (1, 2529):')
    print(f'  _scaled_mm: {ref_fp8[r,c].item():.6f}')
    print(f'  bf16 cuBLAS: {ref_bf16[r,c].item():.6f}')
    print(f'  f32: {ref_f32[r,c].item():.6f}')
except Exception as e:
    print(f'_scaled_mm failed: {e}')

import torch

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
K = 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
a = torch.randn(1, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
b = torch.randn(1, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')

# Try different K-tile sizes to see which matches cuBLAS
ref = (a @ b.T)[0, 0]

for tile_k in [2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64, 128, 256]:
    # Simulate tiled f32 accumulation
    accum = torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.float32, device='cuda')
    for k_start in range(0, K, tile_k):
        k_end = min(k_start + tile_k, K)
        a_tile = a[0, k_start:k_end].float()
        b_tile = b[0, k_start:k_end].float()
        accum += (a_tile * b_tile).sum()
    result = accum.to(torch.bfloat16)
    diff = (result - ref).abs().item()
    print(f'tile_k={tile_k:4d}: result={result.item():.6f} diff_from_cublas={diff:.6f}')

            break

import torch

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
M, N, K = 4096, 4096, 4127

torch.manual_seed(42)
x = (torch.rand(M, K) * 8 - 4).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).cuda()
w = torch.randn(N, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16).cuda()

# Reference: direct bf16 matmul
ref = x_bf16 @ w.T

# Try with K padded to multiple of 32
K_padded = ((K + 31) // 32) * 32  # 4128
x_padded = torch.cat([x_bf16, torch.zeros(M, K_padded - K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)], dim=1)
w_padded = torch.cat([w, torch.zeros(N, K_padded - K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)], dim=1)
ref_padded = x_padded @ w_padded.T  # bf16 matmul with padded K

# These should match the original reference (adding zeros doesn't change the result)
diff = (ref - ref_padded).abs()
print(f'Padded K=4128 vs original K=4127: max_diff={diff.max().item():.4f}')
print(f'  mean={diff.mean().item():.6f}')

# Now, let me also try with the original (no padding) using the direct f32:
r, c = 1, 2529

print(f'  Original ref: {ref[r,c].item():.6f}')
print(f'  Padded ref: {ref_padded[r,c].item():.6f}')

x_padded2 = torch.cat([x_bf16, torch.zeros(M, K_padded2 - K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)], dim=1)
w_padded2 = torch.cat([w, torch.zeros(N, K_padded2 - K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)], dim=1)
ref_padded2 = x_padded2 @ w_padded2.T

diff2 = (ref - ref_padded2).abs()
print(f'\\nPadded K=4160: max_diff={diff2.max().item():.4f}')
print(f'Element (1, 2529): padded={ref_padded2[r,c].item():.6f}')
