import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype, check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[2]  # M=32, N=8192, K=8192
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(123)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(123)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    print(f'ref_out dtype: {ref_out.dtype}')
    print(f'ref_out shape: {ref_out.shape}')
    print(f'NaN in ref: {torch.isnan(ref_out).any().item()}')
    print(f'NaN in sol: {torch.isnan(sol_out).any().item()}')
    print(f'Inf in ref: {torch.isinf(ref_out).any().item()}')
    print(f'Inf in sol: {torch.isinf(sol_out).any().item()}')
    
    merged = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, merged)
    print(f'tol: {tol}')
    
    ok, msg = check_correctness(
        ref_out, sol_out,
        dtype=ref_out.dtype,
        override=merged,
    )
    print(f'check_correctness: {msg}')
    
    # Manual check
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    max_diff = diff.max().item()
    max_allowed = (tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()).max().item()
    print(f'max_diff: {max_diff}')
    print(f'max_allowed: {max_allowed}')
    
    # Check if allclose works
    allclose = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'allclose: {allclose}')
    
    # Manual allclose check
    allowed = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad = diff > allowed
    print(f'bad elements: {bad.sum().item()}/{bad.numel()}')
    
    if bad.sum().item() == 0 and not allclose:
        # Maybe the issue is with large values
        worst_flat = diff.argmax().item()
        wr = worst_flat // ref_out.shape[1]
        wc = worst_flat % ref_out.shape[1]
        print(f'Worst: ({wr}, {wc}) ref={ref_out[wr,wc].item()} sol={sol_out[wr,wc].item()} diff={diff[wr,wc].item()} allowed={allowed[wr,wc].item()}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[2]
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(123)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(123)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    merged = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, merged)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    diff = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    
    # Standard allclose
    close1 = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'Standard allclose: {close1}')
    
    # Allclose with swapped order
    close2 = torch.allclose(sol_f, ref_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'Swapped allclose: {close2}')
    
    # Manual check: all elements
    allowed1 = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_f.abs()
    bad1 = diff > allowed1
    print(f'Bad (using sol for rtol): {bad1.sum().item()}/{bad1.numel()}')
    
    allowed2 = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    bad2 = diff > allowed2
    print(f'Bad (using ref for rtol): {bad2.sum().item()}/{bad2.numel()}')
    
    # Check worst elements by diff
    worst_flat = diff.argmax().item()
    wr = worst_flat // ref_out.shape[1]
    wc = worst_flat % ref_out.shape[1]
    print(f'Worst diff: ({wr}, {wc}) diff={diff[wr,wc].item():.6f} ref={ref_f[wr,wc].item():.6f} sol={sol_f[wr,wc].item():.6f}')
    print(f'  allowed (sol): {allowed1[wr,wc].item():.6f}')
    print(f'  allowed (ref): {allowed2[wr,wc].item():.6f}')
    
    # Check with element-wise allclose
    element_close = diff <= tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_f.abs()
    print(f'All pass element-wise (sol ref): {element_close.all().item()}')
    
    element_close2 = diff <= tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * ref_f.abs()
    print(f'All pass element-wise (ref ref): {element_close2.all().item()}')
    
    # Try with more strict: check the exact allclose behavior
    # allclose checks: |self - other| <= atol + rtol * |other|
    # where self=ref_f, other=sol_f
    rhs = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_f.abs()
    lhs = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    all_pass = (lhs <= rhs).all()
    print(f'Element-wise |ref-sol| <= atol + rtol*|sol|: {all_pass.item()}')
    if not all_pass.item():
        n_fail = (lhs > rhs).sum().item()
        print(f'  Failed elements: {n_fail}')
        fail_idx = (lhs > rhs).nonzero(as_tuple=True)
        for i in range(min(5, n_fail)):
            r = fail_idx[0][i].item()
            c = fail_idx[1][i].item()
            print(f'  ({r}, {c}): ref={ref_f[r,c].item():.6f} sol={sol_f[r,c].item():.6f} diff={lhs[r,c].item():.6f} rhs={rhs[r,c].item():.6f}')

import re, sys
from pathlib import Path
import torch
import yaml

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (
    numeric_stress_cases,
    numeric_stress_context,
    tolerance_for_case,
)

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None
print(f'tol_override: {tol_override}')

all_shapes = shapes.SHAPES
for shape_idx, shape in enumerate(all_shapes):
    reference.M = shape['M']
    reference.N = shape['N']
    reference.K = shape['K']
    
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sd = ref_model.state_dict()
    sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)
    
    for seed in (42, 123, 456):
        torch.manual_seed(seed)
        torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
        base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]
        
        for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
            with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
                with torch.no_grad():
                    ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
                    sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
            
            ok, msg = check_correctness(
                ref_out, sol_out,
                dtype=ref_out.dtype,
                override=tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case),
            )
            if not ok:
                print(f'FAIL: shape {shape_idx} {shape} seed {seed} case {case.name}: {msg}')
                sys.exit(1)
    
_emit_framework_label()
print('PASS')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype, check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(123)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(123)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    merged = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, merged)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    
    # Test allclose directly
    ac = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol={tol[\"atol\"]}, rtol={tol[\"rtol\"]}): {ac}')
    
    # Test with different argument orders
    ac2 = torch.allclose(sol_f, ref_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'torch.allclose(sol_f, ref_f, ...): {ac2}')
    
    # Element-wise check for allclose definition
    lhs = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    rhs = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_f.abs()
    all_pass = (lhs <= rhs).all()
    print(f'Element-wise |ref-sol| <= atol + rtol*|sol|: {all_pass.item()}')
    if not all_pass.item():
        n_fail = (lhs > rhs).sum().item()
        print(f'  Fails: {n_fail}')
        fail_idx = (lhs > rhs).nonzero(as_tuple=True)
        for i in range(min(5, n_fail)):
            r = fail_idx[0][i].item()
            c = fail_idx[1][i].item()
            print(f'  ({r},{c}): ref={ref_f[r,c].item():.6f} sol={sol_f[r,c].item():.6f} lhs={lhs[r,c].item():.6f} rhs={rhs[r,c].item():.6f}')

    print(f'  lhs={lhs[0,43].item():.6f} rhs={rhs[0,43].item():.6f}')
    
    # Check fp64 version for numerical issues
    ref_d = ref_out.double()
    sol_d = sol_out.double()
    lhs_d = (ref_d - sol_d).abs()
    rhs_d = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_d.abs()
    all_pass_d = (lhs_d <= rhs_d).all()
    print(f'fp64 element-wise check: {all_pass_d.item()}')
    
    # Direct test: are ref_f and sol_f close with HUGE tolerance?
    ac3 = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=999.0, rtol=0.99)
    print(f'allclose(atol=999, rtol=0.99): {ac3}')
    
    # Check if there are any differences at all
    print(f'\\nAre ref and sol identical? {torch.equal(ref_out, sol_out)}')
    print(f'Max diff: {(ref_f - sol_f).abs().max().item()}')

import torch, sys, yaml
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path.cwd().parents[2]))

import reference, shapes, solution
from src.eval.numeric_stress import (numeric_stress_cases, numeric_stress_context, tolerance_for_case)
from src.eval.correctness import check_correctness

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
meta = yaml.safe_load(Path('problem.yaml').read_text())
tol_override = meta.get('tolerance') or None

shape = shapes.SHAPES[2]
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(123)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(123)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    # EXACTLY what check.py does
    override_val = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    print(f'override={override_val}')
    
    ok, msg = check_correctness(
        ref_out, sol_out,
        dtype=ref_out.dtype,
        override=override_val,
    )
    
    print(f'ok={ok}, msg={msg}')
    
    # Digging into check_correctness inner workings
    from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override_val)
    print(f'tol={tol}')
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    
    # The exact allclose call
    ac = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    print(f'allclose result: {ac}')
    
    if ac:
        print('allclose says OK but check_correctness returned FAIL!')
        print('This means the check_correctness code path differs from my manual test.')
    else:

                    c = idx[1][i].item()

# Track the specific call
call_tracker = {'count': 0, 'fail_info': None}

def debug_check(ref, sol, dtype=None, override=None):
    call_tracker['count'] += 1
    
    # Shape 2, seed 123, case large_input should happen around call 31
    from src.eval.correctness import tolerance_for_dtype
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(dtype, override)
    
    ref_f = ref.float()
    sol_f = sol.float()
    ac = torch.allclose(ref_f, sol_f, atol=tol['atol'], rtol=tol['rtol'])
    
    if not ac:
        call_tracker['fail_info'] = {
            'call': call_tracker['count'],
            'override': override,
            'tol': tol,
            'shape': ref.shape,
            'dtype': dtype,
        }
        # This call will fail check_correctness
        # Let's not let it fail by returning ok
        # Actually let's see what the original returns
        pass
    
    ok, msg = original_check(ref, sol, dtype=dtype, override=override)
    
    if not ok:
        call_tracker['fail_info'] = {
            'call': call_tracker['count'],
            'override': override,
            'tol': tol,
            'shape': ref.shape,
            'dtype': dtype,
            'ok': ok,
            'msg': msg,
        }
        # Debug this specific failure
        print(f'\\nFAIL at call #{call_tracker[\"count\"]}:')
        print(f'  shape={ref.shape}, dtype={dtype}')
        print(f'  override={override}')
        print(f'  tol={tol}')
        print(f'  msg={msg}')

        my_fails = lhs > my_rhs
        print(f'  element-wise fails (ref-based): {my_fails.sum().item()}/{my_fails.numel()}')
        
        # Show the worst element
        max_idx = lhs.argmax().item()
        r = max_idx // ref.shape[1]
        c = max_idx % ref.shape[1]
        print(f'  worst diff: ({r},{c}) ref={ref[r,c].item():.6f} sol={sol[r,c].item():.6f} diff={lhs[r,c].item():.6f}')
        print(f'  rhs (allclose)={rhs[r,c].item():.6f}')
    
    return ok, msg

shape = shapes.SHAPES[2]
reference.M = shape['M']; reference.N = shape['N']; reference.K = shape['K']

init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
sd = ref_model.state_dict()
sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)

torch.manual_seed(123)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(123)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) for t in reference.get_inputs()]

for case in numeric_stress_cases(meta.get('name', '')):
    if case.name != 'large_input':
        continue
    
    with numeric_stress_context(ref_model, sol_model, base_inputs, case) as inputs:
        with torch.no_grad():
            ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
            sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
    
    override = tolerance_for_case(tol_override, case)
    tol = tolerance_for_dtype(ref_out.dtype, override)
    
    ref_f = ref_out.float()
    sol_f = sol_out.float()
    
    lhs = (ref_f - sol_f).abs()
    rhs = tol['atol'] + tol['rtol'] * sol_f.abs()
    fails = lhs > rhs
    
    print(f'Total element-wise fails: {fails.sum().item()}')
    
    if fails.any():
        fail_indices = torch.nonzero(fails)
        print(f'\\nFirst 10 failing elements:')
        for i in range(min(10, len(fail_indices))):
            r, c = fail_indices[i].tolist()
            print(f'  ({r}, {c}): ref={ref_f[r,c].item():.10f} sol={sol_f[r,c].item():.10f} diff={lhs[r,c].item():.10f} rhs={rhs[r,c].item():.10f}')
            # Check: what does |ref-sol| <= atol + rtol*|sol| equal?
            print(f'    |ref-sol|={lhs[r,c].item():.10f} <= atol={tol[\"atol\"]} + rtol={tol[\"rtol\"]}*|sol|={tol[\"rtol\"]*sol_f[r,c].abs().item():.10f} = {rhs[r,c].item():.10f}')
" 2>&1
